trường, tạm ngưng/kích hoạt, quản lý gói dịch vụ |\n| Quản lý người dùng | CRUD người dùng với phân quyền: SUPER_ADMIN, STAFF, TEACHER |\n| Tiếp nhận học sinh | Thêm HS với kiểm tra tuổi (QD1) và sĩ `STAFF` | Nhân viên giáo vụ | Quản lý HS, lớp, điểm, PH |\n| `TEACHER` | Giáo viên | Xem/nhập điểm lớp được phân công |\n| `STUDENT` | Học sinh | Xem điểm cá nhân |\n| `PARENT` | Phụ huynh | Xem điểm con em được liên kết |\n\n## Tech Stack\n\n### Backend\n- **Node.js** + **Express.js 5**\n- **Prisma ORM** + **PostgreSQL**\n- **JWT** (httpOnly cookie, SameSite=Lax) authentication\n- **bcryptjs** password hashing\n- **express-validator** input validation\n- **helmet** security headers (CSP, X-Content-Type-Options)\n- **express-rate-limit** rate limiting\n- **LRU cache** for user/settings performance optimization\n- **ExcelJS** for Excel export, **json2csv** for CSV export (with formula injection prevention)\n\n### Frontend\n- **Next.js 14** (App Router, TypeScript)\n- **Tailwind CSS** (custom theme)\n- **Zustand** (state management, sessionStorage persistence)\n- **React Hook Form** + **Zod** (form validation)\n- **Axios** (API client with interceptors, blob error handling)\n- **Lucide React** (icons)\n\n### DevOps\n- **Docker** + **Docker Compose**\n- **PostgreSQL 16**\n\n---\n\n## Cài đặt & Chạy\n\n### Yêu cầu\n\n- **Docker** + **Docker Compose** (bắt buộc cho PostgreSQL)\n- **Node.js** >= 18\n- **npm**\n\n---\n\n### 🚀 Development — Chạy nhanh (copy & paste)\n\n#### Bước 1: Clone repo\n\n```bash\ngit clone <repo-url> cloudschool\ncd cloudschool\n```\n\n#### Bước 2: Tạo file cấu hình môi trường\n\n**Linux / macOS:**\n```bash\ncp backend/.env.example backend/.env\ncp frontend/.env.example frontend/.env.local\n```\n\n**Windows (PowerShell):**\n```powershell\nCopy-Item backend/.env.example backend/.env\nCopy-Item frontend/.env.example frontend/.env.local\n```\n\n> File `.env.example` đã có sẵn giá trị mặc định khớp với `docker-compose.dev.yml`, **không cần chỉnh sửa gì** nếu chạy local.\n\n#### Bước 3: Khởi động PostgreSQL bằng Docker\n\n```bash\ndocker-compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d\n```\n\n> PostgreSQL 16 sẽ chạy trên port `5432` với user `postgres`, password `postgres123`, database `cloudschool`.\n\n#### Bước 4: Cài dependencies & khởi tạo database\n\n```bash\n# Cài packages cho backend\ncd Kiến trúc tổng quan\n\n### Multi-Tenant SaaS Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                    Frontend (Next.js 14)                 │\n│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌────────────────────────┐ │\n│  │  Login   │  │ Register │  │   Dashboard (6 roles)  │ │\n│  │  Portal  │  │  School  │  │   Protected Routes     │ │\n│  └────┬─────┘  └────┬─────┘  └────────┬───────────────┘ │\n│       │              │                 │                  │\n│       └──────────────┼─────────────────┘                  │\n│                      │ Axios (httpOnly cookie)            │\n└──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┘\n                       │\n┌──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┐\n│                Backend (Express.js 5)                    │\n│  ┌───────────┐  ┌────┴────┐  ┌──────────────────────┐  │\n│  │   Auth    │  │ Routes  │  │    Middleware         │  │\n│  │  (JWT)    │  │  (13)   │  │ auth · tenantGuard   │  │\n│  └───────────┘  └─────────┘  └──────────────────────┘  │\n│                      │                                   │\n│              ┌───────┴───────┐                           │\n│              │  Prisma ORM   │                           │\n│              └───────┬───────┘                           │\n└──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┘\n                       │\n┌──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┐\n│              PostgreSQL Database                         │\n│     Shared DB — tenant_id isolation per row              │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Mô hình Multi-Tenant\n\n- **Shared Database**: Tất cả trường dùng chung 1 DB PostgreSQL\n- **Row-Level Isolation**: Mỗi record có `tenantId` (FK → Tenant)\n- **TenantGuard Middleware**: Tự động inject `tenantId` vào mọi query\n- **Platform Admin**: Không có `tenantId`, truy vấn cross-tenant\n\n---\n\n## 2. Authentication & Authorization\n\n### 2.1 Luồng đăng nhập\n\n```\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                  LOGIN PAGE                           │\n│                                                      │\n│  ┌──────────────────┐   ┌─────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │  School Login     │   │  Platform Admin Toggle  │  │\n│  │  - Email          │   │  (khi bật: ẩn mã trường│  │\n│  │  - Password       │   │   chỉ cần email + pw)  │  │\n│  │  - Mã trường (*)  │   │                         │  │\n│  └────────┬─────────┘   └────────┬────────────────┘  │\n│           │                       │                    │\n└───────────┼───────────────────────┼────────────────────┘\n            │                       │\n            ▼                       ▼\n    POST /api/auth/login      POST /api/auth/login\n    body: {                   body: {\n      email,                    email,\n      password,                 password\n      tenantCode: \"THPT-DEMO\"  // không có tenantCode\n    }                         }\n            │                       │\n            ▼                       ▼\n    Backend:                  Backend:\n    1. Tìm Tenant by code    1. Tìm User PLATFORM_ADMIN\n    2. Tìm User in tenant    2. Verify password\n    3. Verify password        3. Set JWT cookie\n    4. Set JWT cookie\n```\n\n### 2.2 JWT Cookie-Based Auth\n\n```\nLogin thành công:\n→ Set httpOnly cookie: \"token\" = JWT { id, role, tenantId }\n→ cookie: { httpOnly: true, secure: production, sameSite: 'lax', maxAge: 24h }\n\nMọi request sau:\n→ Browser tự gửi cookie\n→ auth.js middleware: verify JWT → req.user = { id, role, tenantId }\n→ tenantGuard: kiểm tra user.tenantId != null (trừ PLATFORM_ADMIN)\n```\n\n### 2.3 Middleware Chain\n\n```\nRequest → authenticate → authorize(roles) → tenantGuard → Route Handler\n   │           │              │                  │\n   │     Verify JWT     Check role           Check tenantId\n   │     Set req.user   in allowed list      exists (non-admin)\n```\n\n### 2.4 Phân quyền chi tiết\n\n| Endpoint Group | PLATFORM_ADMIN | SUPER_ADMIN | STAFF | TEACHER | STUDENT | PARENT |\n|---------------|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|\n| Admin Schools & Subscriptions | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Users CRUD | ❌ | ✅ | R | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Students CRUD | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | R | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Classes CRUD | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | R | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Subjects & Semesters | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | R | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Score Components | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Score Entry | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅* | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Score View (own) | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ✅ | ❌ |\n| Promotion | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Reports | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Settings & Grades | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Parents CRUD | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| My Children (PH view) | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ✅ |\n| Tenant Info | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |\n\n> *TEACHER chỉ nhập điểm lớp được phân công (TeacherAssignment)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Database Schema\n\n### 3.1 Entity Relationship\n\n```\nSubscriptionPlan 1──N Tenant\nTenant 1──N User\nTenant 1──N Grade 1──N Class\nTenant 1──N Subject 1──N ScoreComponent\nTenant 1──N Semester\nTenant 1──1 TenantSettings\n\nClass N──1 Grade\nClass 1──N TeacherAssignment N──1 User(TEACHER), Subject\nClass 1──N Student\n\nStudent 1──N Score N──1 ScoreComponent, Semester\nStudent 1──N ParentStudent N──1 User(PARENT)\nStudent 1──N Promotion N──1 Semester\n\nUser 1──N ActivityLog\n```\n\n### 3.2 Models chi tiết\n\n#### SubscriptionPlan\n```\nid             Int       @id\nname           String    \"Cơ bản\", \"Nâng cao\", ...\nprice          Float     Giá gói\nstudentLimit   Int       Giới hạn HS\nteacherLimit   Int       Giới hạn GV\nclassLimit     Int       @default(30)\nfeatures       String[]  Danh sách tính năng\nisActive       Boolean   @default(true)\n```\n\n#### Tenant (Trường)\n```\nid          Int     @id\nname        String  Tên trường\ncode        String  @unique  Mã trường (dùng để đăng nhập)\naddress     String?\nphone       String?\nemail       String?\nstatus      Enum    ACTIVE | SUSPENDED | INACTIVE\nplanId      Int?    FK → SubscriptionPlan\n```\n\n#### TenantSettings (Quy định riêng mỗi trường)\n```\ntenantId     Int    @unique FK → Tenant\nminAge       Int    @default(15)  Tuổi tối thiểu (QD1)\nmaxAge       Int    @default(20)  Tuổi tối đa (QD1)\nmaxClassSize Int    @default(40)  Sĩ số tối đa (QD2)\npassScore    Float  @default(5.0) Điểm đạt (QD5)\n```\n\n#### User\n```\nid         Int     @id\nemail      String\npassword   String  (bcrypt hash)\nfullName   String\nrole       Enum    PLATFORM_ADMIN | SUPER_ADMIN | STAFF | TEACHER | STUDENT | PARENT\ntenantId   Int?    null cho PLATFORM_ADMIN\nisActive   Boolean @default(true)\n```\n> Unique constraint: (email, tenantId) — cùng email có thể tồn tại ở trường khác\n\n#### Grade (Khối lớp)\n```\nid        Int     @id\nname      String  \"Khối 10\", \"Khối 11\", \"Khối 12\"\nlevel     Int     10, 11, 12\ntenantId  Int     FK → Tenant\n```\n\n#### Class (Lớp)\n```\nid           Int     @id\nname         String  \"10A1\", \"11B2\"\ngradeId      Int     FK → Grade\ntenantId     Int     FK → Tenant\nacademicYear String  \"2024-2025\"\ncapacity     Int     @default(40)\n```\n> Unique constraint: (name, tenantId, academicYear)\n\n#### Subject (Môn học)\n```\nid          Int      @id\nname        String   \"Toán\", \"Văn\", ...\ndescription String?\ntenantId    Int      FK → Tenant\nisActive    Boolean  @default(true)  (soft delete)\n```\n\n#### ScoreComponent (Đầu điểm)\n```\nid        Int     @id\nname      String  \"Kiểm tra miệng\", \"15 phút\", \"1 tiết\", \"Cuối kỳ\"\nweight    Int     Trọng số (%)  — tổng các đầu điểm ≤ 100\nsubjectId Int     FK → Subject\ntenantId  Int     FK → Tenant\n```\n> **Logic**: Khi tạo/sửa ScoreComponent, backend kiểm tra tổng weight các component cùng subject ≤ 100\n\n#### Semester (Học kỳ)\n```\nid        Int      @id\nname      String   \"Học kỳ 1 - 2024-2025\"\nstartDate DateTime\nendDate   DateTime\ntenantId  Int      FK → Tenant\nisActive  Boolean  @default(true)\n```\n\n#### Student (Học sinh)\n```\nid          Int      @id\nstudentCode String   Auto-gen: \"HS\" + timestamp\nfullName    String\ndateOfBirth DateTime\ngender      Enum     MALE | FEMALE\naddress     String?\nclassId     Int?     FK → Class\ntenantId    Int      FK → Tenant\nparentName  String?\nparentPhone String?\n```\n> **Kiểm tra tuổi (QD1)**: Khi thêm HS, tính tuổi = năm hiện tại - năm sinh. Kiểm tra minAge ≤ tuổi ≤ maxAge\n> **Kiểm tra sĩ số (QD2)**: Đếm HS trong lớp, so với maxClassSize hoặc class.capacity\n\n#### Score (Điểm)\n```\nid               Int     @id\nvalue            Float   Điểm 0-10\nstudentId        Int     FK → Student\nscoreComponentId Int     FK → ScoreComponent\nsemesterId       Int     FK → Semester\ntenantId         Int     FK → Tenant\nisLocked         Boolean @default(false)\n```\n> Unique constraint: (studentId, scoreComponentId, semesterId) — mỗi HS chỉ có 1 điểm mỗi đầu điểm mỗi kỳ\n> Backend dùng `upsert` để insert hoặc update\n\n#### ParentStudent (Liên kết PH-HS)\n```\nparentId     Int     FK → User\nstudentId    Int     FK → Student\nrelationship String  \"Bố\", \"Mẹ\", \"Người giám hộ\"\nisPrimary    Boolean @default(false)\n```\n\n#### Promotion (Xét lên lớp)\n```\nid             Int     @id\nstudentId      Int     FK → Student\nsemesterId     Int     FK → Semester\naverageScore   Float   ĐTB có trọng số\nresult         Enum    PASS | FAIL | RETAKE\ntenantId       Int     FK → Tenant\n```\n\n#### ActivityLog (Nhật ký)\n```\nid        Int      @id\nuserId    Int      FK → User\naction    String   \"CREATE_STUDENT\", \"UPDATE_SCORE\", ...\ndetails   String?  JSON string chi tiết\ntenantId  Int      FK → Tenant\ncreatedAt DateTime\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Hệ thống điểm\n\n### 4.1 Score Components (Đầu điểm)\n\nMỗi môn có N đầu điểm, mỗi đầu điểm có trọng số (weight %). Tổng trọng số ≤ 100%.\n\n**Ví dụ môn Toán:**\n| Đầu điểm | Weight |\n|-----------|--------|\n| Kiểm tra miệng | 10% |\n| KT 15 phút | 20% |\n| KT 1 tiết | 30% |\n| Thi cuối kỳ | 40% |\n| **Tổng** | **100%** |\n\n### 4.2 Công thức tính ĐTB\n\n```\nĐTB = Σ (điểm_i × weight_i) / Σ weight_i\n\nVí dụ:\n  Miệng: 8 × 10 = 80\n  15 phút: 7 × 20 = 140\n  1 tiết: 6 × 30 = 180\n  Cuối kỳ: 7 × 40 = 280\n  ĐTB = (80+140+180+280) / (10+20+30+40) = 680/100 = 6.8\n```\n\n### 4.3 Xét lên lớp (Promotion)\n\n```\nPOST /api/promotion/calculate\nBody: { classId, semesterId }\n\nLogic:\n1. Lấy tất cả HS trong classId\n2. Mỗi HS: lấy tất cả Score trong semesterId\n3. Tính ĐTB theo công thức trên\n4. So sánh với passScore (từ TenantSettings)\n5. Kết quả:\n   - ĐTB >= passScore → PASS\n   - ĐTB < passScore → FAIL\n6. Upsert vào bảng Promotion\n```\n\n### 4.4 Lock/Unlock điểm\n\n- Điểm đã lock không thể sửa/xóa\n- Chỉ SUPER_ADMIN và STAFF có quyền lock/unlock\n- Frontend hiện icon khóa, disable input khi locked\n\n---\n\n## 5. Frontend Architecture\n\n### 5.1 Routing\n\n```\n/login                          → Cổng đăng nhập chung\n/register                       → Đăng ký trường mới\n/(dashboard)/                   → Layout chung (sidebar + menu theo role)\n  ├── dashboard                 → Dashboard tổng hợp (6 roles)\n  ├── admin/schools             → Quản lý trường (PLATFORM_ADMIN only)\n  ├── admin/subscriptions       → Gói dịch vụ (PLATFORM_ADMIN only)\n  ├── users                     → Quản lý người dùng\n  ├── students                  → DS học sinh\n  │   ├── new                   → Thêm HS mới\n  │   └── [id]                  → Chi tiết HS\n  │       └── edit              → Sửa HS\n  ├── classes                   → DS lớp\n  │   └── [id]                  → Chi tiết lớp + phân công GV\n  ├── subjects                  → Môn học + đầu điểm\n  ├── scores                    → Nhập điểm (chọn lớp → môn → kỳ)\n  ├── promotion                 → Xét lên lớp\n  ├── reports                   → Báo cáo\n  ├── parents                   → Quản lý phụ huynh\n  ├── settings                  → Quy định + khối lớp\n  ├── my-children               → PH xem con em\n  │   └── [studentId]/scores    → Điểm con em\n  └── my-scores                 → HS xem điểm cá nhân\n```\n\n### 5.2 Dashboard Sidebar Menu theo Role\n\n| Menu Item | PLATFORM_ADMIN | SUPER_ADMIN | STAFF | TEACHER | STUDENT | PARENT |\n|-----------|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|\n| Dashboard | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |\n| Quản lý Trường | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Gói Dịch vụ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Người dùng | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Học sinh | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Lớp học | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Môn học | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Nhập điểm | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Xét lên lớp | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Báo cáo | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Phụ huynh | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Quy định | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |\n| Con em tôi | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ✅ |\n| Điểm của tôi | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ✅ | ❌ |\n\n### 5.3 State Management (Zustand)\n\n```typescript\n// store/auth.ts\ninterface AuthState {\n  user: User | null        // { id, email, fullName, role, tenantId }\n  token: string | null     // JWT token\n  isAuthenticated: boolean\n  setAuth(user, token)     // set user + token + isAuthenticated\n  logout()                 // clear state, remove cookie\n}\n// Sử dụng persist middleware → lưu vào sessionStorage (đóng tab = logout)\n// storage: createJSONStorage(() => sessionStorage)\n```\n\n### 5.4 API Client (Axios)\n\n```typescript\n// lib/api.ts\nconst api = axios.create({\n  baseURL: NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL,\n  withCredentials: true    // Tự gửi cookie\n})\n\n// Response interceptor: 401 → logout + redirect /login\n// Blob error handling: parse error response from Blob to JSON\n// 18 API modules: authApi, adminApi, userApi, studentApi, classApi,\n//   subjectApi, scoreComponentApi, scoreApi, promotionApi, reportApi,\n//   parentApi, settingsApi, tenantApi, exportApi, monitoringApi,\n//   feeApi, academicYearApi\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Backend Logic chi tiết\n\n### 6.1 Middleware\n\n#### authenticate (auth.js)\n1. Lấy cookie `token` từ request\n2. Verify JWT với `JWT_SECRET`\n3. Query User by id (include tenant)\n4. Set `req.user` = { id, email, fullName, role, tenantId, tenant }\n5. Nếu lỗi → 401 Unauthorized\n\n#### authorize(...roles) (auth.js)\n1. Kiểm tra `req.user.role` in allowed `roles` array\n2. Nếu không → 403 Forbidden\n\n#### tenantGuard (auth.js)\n1. Nếu `req.user.role === 'PLATFORM_ADMIN'` → skip\n2. Nếu `req.user.tenantId` null → 403 \"No tenant access\"\n3. Pass → để route handler dùng `req.user.tenantId`\n\n### 6.2 Error Handling\n\n```\nGlobal errorHandler middleware bắt:\n- Prisma P2002 (Unique constraint) → 409 \"Dữ liệu đã tồn tại\"\n- Prisma P2025 (Record not found) → 404 \"Không tìm thấy\"\n- ValidationError (express-validator) → 400 + details\n- JsonWebTokenError → 401 \"Token không hợp lệ\"\n- TokenExpiredError → 401 \"Token hết hạn\"\n- AppError (custom) → status + message\n- Unknown → 500 \"Internal Server Error\"\n```\n\n### 6.3 Route Logic Highlights\n\n#### Student Admission (POST /api/students)\n```\n1. Validate input (fullName, dateOfBirth, gender required)\n2. Lấy TenantSettings (minAge, maxAge, maxClassSize)\n3. Tính tuổi = năm hiện tại - năm sinh\n4. if (tuổi < minAge || tuổi > maxAge) → 400 \"Không đủ tuổi\"\n5. if (classId) {\n     Đếm HS trong class\n     if (count >= maxClassSize) → 400 \"Lớp đã đầy\"\n   }\n6. Tạo studentCode: \"HS\" + Date.now()\n7. Insert Student\n```\n\n#### Score Entry (POST /api/scores/batch)\n```\n1. Validate array of { studentId, scoreComponentId, semesterId, value }\n2. Mỗi item: kiểm tra 0 ≤ value ≤ 10\n3. Kiểm tra điểm chưa bị lock (isLocked = false)\n4. Dùng Prisma transaction + upsert (insert nếu chưa có, update nếu đã có)\n5. Return danh sách scores đã save\n```\n\n#### Teacher Score Entry (kiểm tra quyền)\n```\n1. TEACHER gọi GET /api/scores/class/:classId\n2. Backend kiểm tra TeacherAssignment: user được phân công cho class này không?\n3. Nếu không → 403 \"Bạn không được phân công cho lớp này\"\n4. Nếu có → trả về bảng điểm\n```\n\n#### Promotion Calculate (POST /api/promotion/calculate)\n```\n1. Input: { classId, semesterId }\n2. Lấy tất cả Students trong class\n3. Lấy tất cả ScoreComponents (đầu điểm) thuộc tenant\n4. Mỗi student:\n   a. Lấy tất cả Scores trong semester\n   b. Tính weighted average:\n      totalWeighted = Σ(score.value * component.weight)\n      totalWeight = Σ(component.weight) — chỉ tính component có score\n      avg = totalWeighted / totalWeight\n   c. So sánh với passScore (TenantSettings)\n   d. Upsert Promotion: PASS hoặc FAIL\n5. Return danh sách kết quả\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Business Rules (Quy định)\n\n| Mã | Quy định | Mặc định | Cấu hình |\n|----|----------|----------|----------|\n| QD1 | Tuổi tiếp nhận HS | 15-20 | Settings → minAge, maxAge |\n| QD2 | Sĩ số tối đa/lớp | 40 | Settings → maxClassSize |\n| QD3 | Khối lớp | 10, 11, 12 | Settings → Grades CRUD |\n| QD4 | Thang điểm | 0-10 | Cố định |\n| QD5 | Điểm đạt | 5.0 | Settings → passScore |\n| QD6 | Đầu điểm | Tùy cấu hình | ScoreComponent CRUD, tổng weight ≤ 100% |\n\n---\n\n## 8. Data Flow Examples\n\n### 8.1 Đăng ký trường mới\n\n```\n1. User truy cập /register\n2. Nhập: Tên trường, Mã trường, Email admin, Tên admin, Password\n3. POST /api/auth/register-school\n4. Backend:\n   a. Kiểm tra mã trường chưa tồn tại\n   b. Tạo Tenant (status: ACTIVE)\n   c. Tạo TenantSettings (default)\n   d. Tạo User (role: SUPER_ADMIN, tenantId)\n   e. Tạo JWT token → set cookie\n5. Redirect → /dashboard\n```\n\n### 8.2 Nhập điểm cho lớp\n\n```\n1. GV/Staff truy cập /scores\n2. Chọn Lớp → Tải DS HS\n3. Chọn Môn → Tải đầu điểm (ScoreComponents)\n4. Chọn Học kỳ\n5. GET /api/scores/class/:classId?subjectId=X&semesterId=Y\n6. Hiện bảng điểm: Rows = HS, Columns = ScoreComponents\n7. Nhập điểm vào ô\n8. Click \"Lưu tất cả\"\n9. POST /api/scores/batch (array of scores)\n10. Backend upsert từng score\n```\n\n### 8.3 Phụ huynh xem điểm con\n\n```\n1. PH đăng nhập (email + mã trường)\n2. Tự động vào /my-children\n3. GET /api/parents/my-children → DS con em (qua ParentStudent)\n4. Click \"Xem điểm\" → /my-children/[studentId]/scores\n5. GET /api/parents/my-children/:studentId/scores?semesterId=X\n6. Hiện bảng điểm + ĐTB\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Security\n\n### 9.1 Authentication\n- Password hash: bcryptjs (10 rounds)\n- JWT: httpOnly cookie, SameSite=Lax, Secure in production\n- Token expiry: 24 hours\n- Logout: clear cookie\n\n### 9.2 Authorization\n- 3-layer: authenticate → authorize(roles) → tenantGuard\n- Role whitelist per endpoint\n- Tenant isolation: query always includes tenantId\n\n### 9.3 Input Validation\n- express-validator cho mọi input\n- Zod schema validation ở frontend\n- Prisma type safety\n\n### 9.4 Other\n- Helmet.js: security headers (CSP, X-Content-Type-Options, etc.)\n- CORS: whitelist CORS_ORIGIN\n- Error handler: không leak stack trace ở production\n- CSV Formula Injection Prevention: escape values starting with `=`, `+`, `-`, `@`\n- X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff on all export responses\n- Content Security Policy: default-src 'self', script-src 'self'\n\n### 9.5 Business Logic Protections\n- Race condition prevention: Serializable isolation level for class capacity checks\n- Student delete guard: blocks deletion if student has promotions, fees, transfers, parent links, enrollments, or scores\n- Fee delete guard: blocks deletion if fee has student payment records\n- Capacity guard: cannot reduce class capacity below current student count\n- Academic year overlap check: prevents overlapping year ranges on create/update\n- Role escalation prevention: only SUPER_ADMIN, STAFF, TEACHER roles allowed via user PUT\n- PassScore range validation: must be within [minScore, maxScore]\n- ScoreComponent-Subject validation: batch score entry validates component belongs to subject\n- Tenant verification: batch score entry verifies all students belong to tenant\n- Max retention scoping: counts failures by academic year (with year string fallback if no academicYearId)\n- Year-end promotion tracking: skipped students (missing grades) are tracked and reported in response\n- Ranking edge case: returns `null` ranking when student not found in classmate averages\n- Cache invalidation: `invalidateUserCache()` called on user disable\n\n---\n\n## 10. Deployment\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n#### Backend (.env)\n```\nPORT=5000\nNODE_ENV=production\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:pass@host:5432/cloudschool\nJWT_SECRET=<random-256-bit-string>\nJWT_EXPIRES_IN=24h\nCORS_ORIGIN=https://your-domain.com\nCOOKIE_SECURE=true          # false cho development\nTZ_OFFSET_HOURS=7           # Timezone offset cho teacher semester check (mặc định UTC+7 Vietnam)\nRATE_LIMIT_BYPASS_SECRET=   # Secret cho automated testing\n```\n\n#### Frontend (.env.local)\n```\nNEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://api.your-domain.com/api\n```\n\n### Docker Production\n\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d --build\ndocker-compose exec backend npx prisma migrate deploy\ndocker-compose exec backend npm run db:seed  # lần đầu\n```\n\n### Ports\n- Frontend: 3000\n- Backend: 5000\n- PostgreSQL: 5432\n"

Parse the JSON from the hook output\n2. Use `AskUserQuestion` with the question data from the JSON\n3. Based on user's selection:\n   - **\"Yes, approve access\"** → Use `bash cat \"filepath\"` to read the file (bash is auto-approved)\n   - **\"No, skip this file\"** → Continue without accessing the file\n\n**Example AskUserQuestion call:**\n```json\n{\n  \"questions\": [{\n    \"question\": \"I need to read \\\".env\\\" which may contain sensitive data. Do you approve?\",\n    \"header\": \"File Access\",\n    \"options\": [\n      { \"label\": \"Yes, approve access\", \"description\": \"Allow reading .env this time\" },\n      { \"label\": \"No, skip this file\", \"description\": \"Continue without accessing this file\" }\n    ],\n    \"multiSelect\": false\n  }]\n}\n```\n\n**IMPORTANT:** Always ask the user via `AskUserQuestion` first. Row-level isolation\"]\n    end\n\n    Login -->|\"Axios (httpOnly cookie)\"| Auth\n    Register -->|\"Axios (httpOnly cookie)\"| Auth\n    Dashboard -->|\"Axios (httpOnly cookie)\"| Routes\n    Auth --> Middleware\n    Routes --> Middleware\n    Middleware --> Prisma\n    Prisma --> Data\n```\n\n## Component Layers\n\n| Layer | Technology | Purpose |\n|-------|------------|---------|\n| **Frontend** | Next.js 14, React, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS | UI, routing, state management |\n| **API Client** | Axios with interceptors | HTTP requests, error handling, 401 redirect |\n| **State Management** | Zustand + sessionStorage | Auth state, user info, tenant context |\n| **Backend API** | Express.js 5, Prisma ORM | REST API, business logic, data access |\n| **Authentication** | JWT + bcryptjs + cookie-parser | Token-based auth, httpOnly cookies |\n| **Database** | PostgreSQL 16 | Shared database with tenant isolation |\n| **DevOps** | Docker, Docker Compose | Container orchestration |\n\n## Key Architectural Decisions\n\n### Shared Database, Row-Level Isolation\n- All tenants share one PostgreSQL database\n- Every row includes `tenantId` foreign key\n- Middleware automatically injects tenant context into queries\n- Platform Admin bypasses tenant scoping\n\n### JWT Cookie-Based Authentication\n- Tokens stored in httpOnly, SameSite=Lax cookies\n- Browser auto-sends cookies with requests\n- No XSS vulnerability from localStorage token access\n- 24-hour token expiry\n\n### Role-Based Access Control\n- 6 distinct roles with different permissions\n- Middleware chain: authenticate → authorize → tenantGuard\n- UI dynamically shows/hides features based on role\n\n## Related\n- [Multi-Tenant Model](multi-tenant-model.md)\n- [Technology Stack](tech-stack.md)\n- [Authentication Overview](../authentication/overview.md)\n",

Shared_Database[\"Shared PostgreSQL Database\"]\n        T1[\"Tenant 1 Data\"]\n        T2[\"Tenant 2 Data\"]\n        T3[\"Tenant 3 Data\"]\n    end\n\n    School1[\"School A\"] -->|\"tenantId: 1\"| T1\n    School2[\"School B\"] -->|\"tenantId: 2\"| T2\n    School3[\"School C\"] -->|\"tenantId: 3\"| T3\n    PlatformAdmin[\"Platform Admin\"] -.->|\"No tenantId\"| T1\n    PlatformAdmin -.->|\"No tenantId\"| T2\n    PlatformAdmin -.->|\"No tenantId\"| T3\n```\n\n## Tenant Isolation Strategy\n\n### Row-Level Security\nEvery business entity includes a `tenantId` foreign key:\n- Students, Classes, Subjects, Scores, Promotions\n- Users, ActivityLogs, Fees, TeacherAssignments\n- TransferHistories, ClassEnrollments\n\n### TenantGuard Middleware\n```javascript\n// backend/src/middleware/auth.js\nconst tenantGuard = (req, res, next) => {\n  if (req.user.role === 'PLATFORM_ADMIN') return next()\n  if (!req.tenantId) {\n    return next(new AppError('Tenant context required', 403, 'NO_TENANT'))\n  }\n  next()\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Platform Admin: bypasses tenant scoping (cross-tenant queries)\n- All other roles: must have `tenantId`, queries scoped to tenant\n\n### Tenant Context Injection\nAfter authentication, `req.tenantId` is automatically set from user's tenant affiliation:\n```javascript\nreq.tenantId = user.tenantId\n```\n\nAll route handlers use `req.tenantId` in Prisma queries:\n```javascript\nconst students = await prisma.student.findMany({\n  where: { tenantId: req.tenantId }\n})\n```\n\n## Tenant Entity\n\n```prisma\nmodel Tenant {\n  id          String       @id @default(uuid())\n  name        String       // School name\n  code        String       @unique  // Login code (e.g., \"THPT-DEMO\")\n  status      TenantStatus @default(ACTIVE)  // ACTIVE | SUSPENDED | INACTIVE\n  planId      String?      // FK → SubscriptionPlan\n  // Relations\n  users             User[]\n  students          Student[]\n  classes           Class[]\n  // ... 15+ more relations\n}\n```\n\n## Tenant Settings\n\nEach tenant has configurable settings:\n```prisma\nmodel TenantSettings {\n  tenantId     String  @unique FK → Tenant\n  minAge       Int     @default(15)   // QD1\n  maxAge       Int     @default(20)   // QD1\n  maxClassSize Int     @default(40)   // QD2\n  passScore    Float   @default(5.0)  // QD5\n  // ... more settings\n}\n```\n\n**Cached**: LRU cache (100 entries, 5min TTL) for performance.\n\n## Subscription Plans\n\nTenants are associated with subscription plans that define limits:\n```prisma\nmodel SubscriptionPlan {\n  id           String   @id\n  name         String   @unique  // \"Cơ bản\", \"Nâng cao\"\n  studentLimit Int      @default(100)\n  teacherLimit Int      @default(20)\n  classLimit   Int      @default(30)\n  features     String[] // Feature flags\n  isActive     Boolean  @default(true)\n}\n```\n\n## Tenant Lifecycle\n\n1. **Registration**: School self-registers via `/register`\n2. **Creation**: Creates Tenant + TenantSettings + default Grades + SUPER_ADMIN user\n3. **Active**: Tenant operates normally (ACTIVE status)\n4. **Suspend**: Platform Admin can suspend (SUSPENDED status, users can't login)\n5. **Delete**: Platform Admin can delete (removes all associated data via Cascade)\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n- **Cross-tenant queries prevented**: Every query includes `tenantId` filter\n- **Cascade deletes**: Deleting a tenant removes all associated data\n- **Settings isolation**: Each tenant has independent settings\n- **Code uniqueness**: Tenant `code` is unique across all tenants\n\n## Related\n- [Architecture Overview](overview.md)\n- [Tenant Isolation Security](../security/tenant-isolation.md)\n- [Login Flows](../authentication/login-flows.md)\n",
              "file_path": "C:\\Users\\ChuHai\\Documents\\CloudSchool\\docs\\system\\architecture\\multi-tenant-model.md"
            }
          }

Integration\n- Always follow the plan given by `planner` agent\n- Ensure seamless integration with existing code\n- Follow API contracts precisely\n- Maintain backward compatibility\n- Document breaking changes\n- Delegate to `docs-manager` agent to update docs in `./docs` directory if any.\n\n#### 5. Debugging\n- When a user report bugs or issues on the server or a CI/CD pipeline, delegate to `debugger` agent to run tests and analyze the summary report.\n- Read the summary report from `debugger` agent and implement the fix.\n- Delegate to `tester` agent to run tests and analyze the summary report.\n- If the `tester` agent reports failed tests, fix them follow the recommendations and repeat from the **Step 3**.\n\n#### 6. Visual Explanations\nWhen explaining complex code, protocols, or architecture:\n- **When to use:** User asks \"explain\", \"how does X work\", \"visualize\", or topic has 3+ interacting components\n- Use `/preview --explain <topic>` to generate visual explanation with ASCII + Mermaid\n- Use `/preview --diagram <topic>` for architecture and data flow diagrams\n- Use `/preview --slides <topic>` for step-by-step walkthroughs\n- Use `/preview --ascii <topic>` for terminal-friendly output only\n- **Plan context:** Visuals save to plan folder from `## Plan Context` hook injection; if none, uses `plans/visuals/`\n- Auto-opens in browser via markdown-novel-viewer with Mermaid rendering\n- See `development-rules.md` → \"Visual Aids\" section for additional guidance\n"
            }
          }

Hệ thống sử dụng mã hóa AES-256, tuân thủ tiêu chuẩn bảo mật quốc tế.\" />\n      <FAQItem question=\"Tôi có thể dùng thử trước khi mua không?\" answer=\"Có! Gói Miễn phí cho phép tối đa 200 học sinh với đầy đủ tính năng. Gói Chuyên nghiệp có 14 ngày dùng thử miễn phí, không cần thẻ tín dụng.\" />\n      <FAQItem question=\"Phụ huynh có cần trả phí để xem điểm không?\" answer=\"Không. Tài khoản phụ huynh hoàn toàn miễn phí, được tạo tự động khi nhà trường thêm thông tin học sinh vào hệ thống.\" />\n      <FAQItem question=\"Hệ thống có hỗ trợ mobile không?\" answer=\"Có. CloudSchool tương thích hoàn toàn với điện thoại, máy tính bảng. Phụ huynh và giáo viên có thể sử dụng mọi tính năng trên mobile.\" />\n      <FAQItem question=\"Tôi có thể xuất báo cáo ra Excel/PDF không?\" answer=\"Gói Chuyên nghiệp và Enterprise hỗ trợ xuất báo cáo đa định dạng (Excel, PDF, CSV). Links, Contact info\n- Add a subtle gradient glow behind the footer logo\n\n---\n\n## Phase 3: IntersectionObserver Upgrade\n\nReplace the existing per-section `useInView` pattern with a more robust **IntersectionObserver-based** approach that supports:\n- Stagger animations for child elements\n- Once-only triggering (unobserve after visible)\n- Multiple reveal directions (up, left, right, scale)\n\n**Add a new hook:**\n```tsx\nfunction useScrollReveal(options = { threshold: 0.1, rootMargin: '0px 0px -50px 0px' }) {\n  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)\n  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const el = ref.current\n    if (!el) return\n    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(([entry]) => {\n      if (entry.isIntersecting) {\n        setIsVisible(true)\n        observer.unobserve(el)\n      }\n    }, options)\n    observer.observe(el)\n    return () => observer.disconnect()\n  }, [])\n\n  return { ref, isVisible }\n}\n```\n\nKeep the old `useInView` for backward compatibility with `AnimatedCounter`.\n\n---\n\n## Phase 4: Implementation Order\n\n| Phase | File | Estimated Lines | Action |\n|-------|------|----------------|--------|\n| 1 | `tailwind.config.js` | ~60 new | Add animations, keyframes, utilities |\n| 2 | `globals.css` | ~80 new | Add glass, reveal, particle, wave CSS |\n| 3 | `page.tsx` top | ~120 | New imports, FAQItem, TestimonialCard, CSSDashboardMockup, useScrollReveal hook |\n| 4 | `page.tsx` navbar | 0 net change | Polish classes only |\n| 5 | `page.tsx` hero | +60 | Add particles, mockup, scroll indicator, gradient text |\n| 6 | `page.tsx` stats | +20 | Add icons, glass cards, dot pattern |\n| 7 | `page.tsx` features | +15 | Glassmorphism, arrow indicators |\n| 8 | `page.tsx` how-it-works | +10 | Pulse rings, shimmer line |\n| 9 | `page.tsx` **NEW** Trusted By | +30 | Marquee logo bar |\n| 10 | `page.tsx` multi-tenant | +10 | Polish only |\n| 11 | `page.tsx` **NEW** Testimonials | +50 | Testimonial carousel |\n| 12 | `page.tsx` pricing | +15 | Gradient border, polish |\n| 13 | `page.tsx` **NEW** FAQ | +40 | FAQ accordion |\n| 14 | `page.tsx` CTA | +15 | Glass card, particles |\n| 15 | `page.tsx` footer | +20 | 3-column layout, wave |\n| | **Total page.tsx** | **~900-1000** | |\n\n---\n\n## Risk Mitigation\n\n| Risk | Mitigation |\n|------|-----------|\n| Auth redirect breaks | Keep `if (isAuthenticated) return null` and `router.push('/dashboard')` unchanged |\n| Mobile menu breaks | Keep mobile menu JSX identical, only add visual polish |\n| Scroll behavior breaks | Keep `scrolled` state and navbar logic unchanged |\n| Animation performance | Use `transform` and `opacity` only (GPU-accelerated), avoid layout thrashing |\n| Page size | All additions are CSS/JSX, no images or external assets needed |\n| Cross-browser | CSS `@property` for animated borders works in Chrome/Edge; Firefox fallback is static gradient |\n| `@property` support | Only Chrome 85+, Edge 85+. For Firefox, the gradient border falls back to static — acceptable degradation |\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Visual Impact\n\n| Area | Before | After |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Hero | Dark with blobs | Dark with blobs + particles + dashboard mockup + scroll indicator + shimmer gradient text |\n| Stats | Plain grid | Glass cards with icons, dot pattern, hover lift |\n| Features | White cards with colored icons | Glassmorphism cards, gradient borders on hover, slide-in arrows |\n| How It Works | Simple numbered steps | Pulse rings, shimmer connection line, step icons |\n| Multi-Tenant | Split layout + terminal | Same + wave dividers, glow effects |\n| **NEW: Trusted By** | — | Auto-scrolling marquee of school names |\n| **NEW: Testimonials** | — | Auto-scrolling testimonial cards with star ratings |\n| Pricing | 3-column cards | Animated gradient border on featured, hover glow |\n| **NEW: FAQ** | — | Accordion with smooth expand/collapse |\n| CTA | Dark with grid | Dark with grid + glass card wrapper + particles |\n| Footer | Simple single row | 3-column with wave divider, contact info |\n\nThis plan delivers a **dramatic visual upgrade** — transforming the page from a standard SaaS template into a premium, animation-rich landing experience — while maintaining 100% backward compatibility with existing functionality."

Contains 50+ styles, 97 color palettes, 57 font pairings, 99 UX guidelines, and 25 chart types across 9 technology stacks. Searchable database with priority-based recommendations.\n\n## When to Apply\n\nReference these guidelines when:\n- Designing new UI components or pages\n- Choosing color palettes and typography\n- Reviewing code for UX issues\n- Building landing pages or dashboards\n- Implementing accessibility requirements\n\n## Rule Categories by Priority\n\n| Priority | Category | Impact | Domain |\n|----------|----------|--------|--------|\n| 1 | Accessibility | CRITICAL | `ux` |\n| 2 | Touch & Interaction | CRITICAL | `ux` |\n| 3 | Performance | HIGH | `ux` |\n| 4 | Layout & Responsive | HIGH | `ux` |\n| 5 | Typography & Color | MEDIUM | `typography`, `color` |\n| 6 | Animation | MEDIUM | `ux` |\n| 7 | Style Selection | MEDIUM | `style`, `product` |\n| 8 | Charts & Data | LOW | `chart` |\n\n## Quick Reference\n\n### 1. Accessibility (CRITICAL)\n\n- `color-contrast` - Minimum 4.5:1 ratio for normal text\n- `focus-states` - Visible focus rings on interactive elements\n- `alt-text` - Descriptive alt text for meaningful images\n- `aria-labels` - aria-label for icon-only buttons\n- `keyboard-nav` - Tab order matches visual order\n- `form-labels` - Use label with for attribute\n\n### 2. Touch & Interaction (CRITICAL)\n\n- `touch-target-size` - Minimum 44x44px touch targets\n- `hover-vs-tap` - Use click/tap for primary interactions\n- `loading-buttons` - Disable button during async operations\n- `error-feedback` - Clear error messages near problem\n- `cursor-pointer` - Add cursor-pointer to clickable elements\n\n### 3. Performance (HIGH)\n\n- `image-optimization` - Use WebP, srcset, lazy loading\n- `reduced-motion` - Check prefers-reduced-motion\n- `content-jumping` - Reserve space for async content\n\n### 4. Layout & Responsive (HIGH)\n\n- `viewport-meta` - width=device-width initial-scale=1\n- `readable-font-size` - Minimum 16px body text on mobile\n- `horizontal-scroll` - Ensure content fits viewport width\n- `z-index-management` - Define z-index scale (10, 20, 30, 50)\n\n### 5. Typography & Color (MEDIUM)\n\n- `line-height` - Use 1.5-1.75 for body text\n- `line-length` - Limit to 65-75 characters per line\n- `font-pairing` - Match heading/body font personalities\n\n### 6. Animation (MEDIUM)\n\n- `duration-timing` - Use 150-300ms for micro-interactions\n- `transform-performance` - Use transform/opacity, not width/height\n- `loading-states` - Skeleton screens or spinners\n\n### 7. Style Selection (MEDIUM)\n\n- `style-match` - Match style to product type\n- `consistency` - Use same style across all pages\n- `no-emoji-icons` - Use SVG icons, not emojis\n\n### 8. Charts & Data (LOW)\n\n- `chart-type` - Match chart type to data type\n- `color-guidance` - Use accessible color palettes\n- `data-table` - Provide table alternative for accessibility\n\n## How to Use\n\nSearch specific domains using the CLI tool below.\n\n---\n\n## Prerequisites\n\nCheck if Python is installed:\n\n```bash\npython3 --version || python --version\n```\n\nIf Python is not installed, install it based on user's OS:\n\n**macOS:**\n```bash\nbrew install python3\n```\n\n**Ubuntu/Debian:**\n```bash\nsudo apt update && sudo apt install python3\n```\n\n**Windows:**\n```powershell\nwinget install Python.Python.3.12\n```\n\n---\n\n## How to Use This Skill\n\nWhen user requests UI/UX work (design, build, create, implement, review, fix, improve), follow this workflow:\n\n### Step 1: Analyze User Requirements\n\nExtract key information from user request:\n- **Product type**: SaaS, e-commerce, portfolio, dashboard, landing page, etc.\n- **Style keywords**: minimal, playful, professional, elegant, dark mode, etc.\n- **Industry**: healthcare, fintech, gaming, education, etc.\n- **Stack**: React, Vue, Next.js, or default to `html-tailwind`\n\n### Step 2: Generate Design System (REQUIRED)\n\n**Always start with `--design-system`** to get comprehensive recommendations with reasoning:\n\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"<product_type> <industry> <keywords>\" --design-system [-p \"Project Name\"]\n```\n\nThis command:\n1. Searches 5 domains in parallel (product, style, color, landing, typography)\n2. Applies reasoning rules from `ui-reasoning.csv` to select best matches\n3. Returns complete design system: pattern, style, colors, typography, effects\n4. Includes anti-patterns to avoid\n\n**Example:**\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"beauty spa wellness service\" --design-system -p \"Serenity Spa\"\n```\n\n### Step 3: Supplement with Detailed Searches (as needed)\n\nAfter getting the design system, use domain searches to get additional details:\n\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"<keyword>\" --domain <domain> [-n <max_results>]\n```\n\n**When to use detailed searches:**\n\n| Need | Domain | Example |\n|------|--------|---------|\n| More style options | `style` | `--domain style \"glassmorphism dark\"` |\n| Chart recommendations | `chart` | `--domain chart \"real-time dashboard\"` |\n| UX best practices | `ux` | `--domain ux \"animation accessibility\"` |\n| Alternative fonts | `typography` | `--domain typography \"elegant luxury\"` |\n| Landing structure | `landing` | `--domain landing \"hero social-proof\"` |\n\n### Step 4: Stack Guidelines (Default: html-tailwind)\n\nGet implementation-specific best practices. If user doesn't specify a stack, **default to `html-tailwind`**.\n\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"<keyword>\" --stack html-tailwind\n```\n\nAvailable stacks: `html-tailwind`, `react`, `nextjs`, `vue`, `svelte`, `swiftui`, `react-native`, `flutter`, `shadcn`\n\n---\n\n## Search Reference\n\n### Available Domains\n\n| Domain | Use For | Example Keywords |\n|--------|---------|------------------|\n| `product` | Product type recommendations | SaaS, e-commerce, portfolio, healthcare, beauty, service |\n| `style` | UI styles, colors, effects | glassmorphism, minimalism, dark mode, brutalism |\n| `typography` | Font pairings, Google Fonts | elegant, playful, professional, modern |\n| `color` | Color palettes by product type | saas, ecommerce, healthcare, beauty, fintech, service |\n| `landing` | Page structure, CTA strategies | hero, hero-centric, testimonial, pricing, social-proof |\n| `chart` | Chart types, library recommendations | trend, comparison, timeline, funnel, pie |\n| `ux` | Best practices, anti-patterns | animation, accessibility, z-index, loading |\n| `react` | React/Next.js performance | waterfall, bundle, suspense, memo, rerender, cache |\n| `web` | Web interface guidelines | aria, focus, keyboard, semantic, virtualize |\n| `prompt` | AI prompts, CSS keywords | (style name) |\n\n### Available Stacks\n\n| Stack | Focus |\n|-------|-------|\n| `html-tailwind` | Tailwind utilities, responsive, a11y (DEFAULT) |\n| `react` | State, hooks, performance, patterns |\n| `nextjs` | SSR, routing, images, API routes |\n| `vue` | Composition API, Pinia, Vue Router |\n| `svelte` | Runes, stores, SvelteKit |\n| `swiftui` | Views, State, Navigation, Animation |\n| `react-native` | Components, Navigation, Lists |\n| `flutter` | Widgets, State, Layout, Theming |\n| `shadcn` | shadcn/ui components, theming, forms, patterns |\n\n---\n\n## Example Workflow\n\n**User request:** \"Làm landing page cho dịch vụ chăm sóc da chuyên nghiệp\"\n\n### Step 1: Analyze Requirements\n- Product type: Beauty/Spa service\n- Style keywords: elegant, professional, soft\n- Industry: Beauty/Wellness\n- Stack: html-tailwind (default)\n\n### Step 2: Generate Design System (REQUIRED)\n\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"beauty spa wellness service elegant\" --design-system -p \"Serenity Spa\"\n```\n\n**Output:** Complete design system with pattern, style, colors, typography, effects, and anti-patterns.\n\n### Step 3: Supplement with Detailed Searches (as needed)\n\n```bash\n# Get UX guidelines for animation and accessibility\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"animation accessibility\" --domain ux\n\n# Get alternative typography options if needed\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"elegant luxury serif\" --domain typography\n```\n\n### Step 4: Stack Guidelines\n\n```bash\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"layout responsive form\" --stack html-tailwind\n```\n\n**Then:** Synthesize design system + detailed searches and implement the design.\n\n---\n\n## Output Formats\n\nThe `--design-system` flag supports two output formats:\n\n```bash\n# ASCII box (default) - best for terminal display\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"fintech crypto\" --design-system\n\n# Markdown - best for documentation\npython3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py \"fintech crypto\" --design-system -f markdown\n```\n\n---\n\n## Tips for Better Results\n\n1. **Be specific with keywords** - \"healthcare SaaS dashboard\" > \"app\"\n2. **Search multiple times** - Different keywords reveal different insights\n3. **Combine domains** - Style + Typography + Color = Complete design system\n4. **Always check UX** - Search \"animation\", \"z-index\", \"accessibility\" for common issues\n5. **Use stack flag** - Get implementation-specific best practices\n6. **Iterate** - If first search doesn't match, try different keywords\n\n---\n\n## Common Rules for Professional UI\n\nThese are frequently overlooked issues that make UI look unprofessional:\n\n### Icons & Visual Elements\n\n| Rule | Do | Don't |\n|------|----|----- |\n| **No emoji icons** | Use SVG icons (Heroicons, Lucide, Simple Icons) | Use emojis like 🎨 🚀 ⚙️ as UI icons |\n| **Stable hover states** | Use color/opacity transitions on hover | Use scale transforms that shift layout |\n| **Correct brand logos** | Research official SVG from Simple Icons | Guess or use incorrect logo paths |\n| **Consistent icon sizing** | Use fixed viewBox (24x24) with w-6 h-6 | Mix different icon sizes randomly |\n\n### Interaction & Cursor\n\n| Rule | Do | Don't |\n|------|----|----- |\n| **Cursor pointer** | Add `cursor-pointer` to all clickable/hoverable cards | Leave default cursor on interactive elements |\n| **Hover feedback** | Provide visual feedback (color, shadow, border) | No indication element is interactive |\n| **Smooth transitions** | Use `transition-colors duration-200` | Instant state changes or too slow (>500ms) |\n\n### Light/Dark Mode Contrast\n\n| Rule | Do | Don't |\n|------|----|----- |\n| **Glass card light mode** | Use `bg-white/80` or higher opacity | Use `bg-white/10` (too transparent) |\n| **Text contrast light** | Use `#0F172A` (slate-900) for text | Use `#94A3B8` (slate-400) for body text |\n| **Muted text light** | Use `#475569` (slate-600) minimum | Use gray-400 or lighter |\n| **Border visibility** | Use `border-gray-200` in light mode | Use `border-white/10` (invisible) |\n\n### Layout & Spacing\n\n| Rule | Do | Don't |\n|------|----|----- |\n| **Floating navbar** | Add `top-4 left-4 right-4` spacing | Stick navbar to `top-0 left-0 right-0` |\n| **Content padding** | Account for fixed navbar height | Let content hide behind fixed elements |\n| **Consistent max-width** | Use same `max-w-6xl` or `max-w-7xl` | Mix different container widths |\n\n---\n\n## Pre-Delivery Checklist\n\nBefore delivering UI code, verify these items:\n\n### Visual Quality\n- [ ] No emojis used as icons (use SVG instead)\n- [ ] All icons from consistent icon set (Heroicons/Lucide)\n- [ ] Brand logos are correct (verified from Simple Icons)\n- [ ] Hover states don't cause layout shift\n- [ ] Use theme colors directly (bg-primary) not var() wrapper\n\n### Interaction\n- [ ] All clickable elements have `cursor-pointer`\n- [ ] Hover states provide clear visual feedback\n- [ ] Transitions are smooth (150-300ms)\n- [ ] Focus states visible for keyboard navigation\n\n### Light/Dark Mode\n- [ ] Light mode text has sufficient contrast (4.5:1 minimum)\n- [ ] Glass/transparent elements visible in light mode\n- [ ] Borders visible in both modes\n- [ ] Test both modes before delivery\n\n### Layout\n- [ ] Floating elements have proper spacing from edges\n- [ ] No content hidden behind fixed navbars\n- [ ] Responsive at 375px, 768px, 1024px, 1440px\n- [ ] No horizontal scroll on mobile\n\n### Accessibility\n- [ ] All images have alt text\n- [ ] Form inputs have labels\n- [ ] Color is not the only indicator\n- [ ] `prefers-reduced-motion` respected\n"
            }

What the Project Is\n\n**Purpose:** \"Virtual Girlfriend\" AI companion web application where users interact with AI-powered virtual romantic partners through real-time chat, with gamification systems (quests, gifts, levels, affection), user-to-user DMs, leaderboards, and subscription monetization.\n\n**Domain:** AI companion / virtual relationship / gamified social\n\n**Target Users:** Vietnamese-speaking users (primary language is Vietnamese) seeking AI companionship with relationship progression mechanics\n\n**Internal codename:** \"Amoura\" (visible in API info endpoint)\n\n**Public domain:** vgfriend.io.vn\n\n---\n\n### 2. Full Tech Stack\n\n| Layer | Technology |\n|-------|-----------|\n| **Frontend** | Next.js 14 (App Router), React 18, TypeScript |\n| **Styling** | TailwindCSS, Tailwind Animate, class-variance-authority, clsx |\n| **UI Components** | Radix UI (13 components: avatar, dialog, dropdown, toast, tabs, etc.) |\n| **Animations** | Framer Motion |\n| **State Management** | Zustand (with persist middleware) |\n| **Data Fetching** | @tanstack/react-query |\n| **Charts** | Chart.js + react-chartjs-2 |\n| **Icons** | Lucide React |\n| **Real-time** | Socket.io Client |\n| **Backend** | Express.js, TypeScript, tsx (dev) |\n| **ORM** | Prisma 5 |\n| **Database** | PostgreSQL 16 |\n| **Cache** | Redis 7 (ioredis) |\n| **AI** | Groq (primary, free), OpenAI-compatible SDK |\n| **Auth** | JWT (access 15min + refresh 7days), bcrypt(12), OTP via email |\n| **Payments** | Stripe (subscriptions, webhooks) |\n| **Storage** | DigitalOcean Spaces (S3-compatible) |\n| **Email** | Nodemailer (SMTP) |\n| **Validation** | Zod |\n| **HTTP Security** | Helmet, CORS, compression |\n| **Rate Limiting** | express-rate-limit (per-IP for public, per-user for authed) |\n| **Logging** | Structured logger with module tags |\n| **Containerization** | Docker + Docker Compose |\n| **Reverse Proxy** | Nginx (SSL, gzip, rate limiting, WebSocket proxy) |\n| **CI/CD** | GitHub Actions (typecheck → build → push GHCR → SSH deploy → migrate → verify) |\n| **Release** | semantic-release (conventional commits, beta on dev, production on main) |\n| **E2E Testing** | Playwright (10 test specs: API + UI) |\n| **Shared Types** | `@vgfriend/shared` (TypeScript types for client/server contract) |\n\n---\n\n### 3. Architecture Overview\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                        NGINX (443/80)                    │\n│  SSL termination, gzip, rate limiting, WS proxy         │\n├──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┤\n│   client:3000        │      server:3001                  │\n│   Next.js 14         │      Express.js + Socket.IO       │\n│   (App Router)       │                                   │\n│                      │  ┌─────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  ┌────────────────┐  │  │  Routes: /api/*             │  │\n│  │ Zustand Stores │  │  │  - auth, users, character   │  │\n│  │ - auth-store   │  │  │  - chat, quests, gifts      │  │\n│  │ - chat-store   │  │  │  - scenes, memories, game   │  │\n│  │ - char-store   │  │  │  - analytics, dm, leaderboard│ │\n│  │ - scene-store  │  │  │  - admin, payment           │  │\n│  │ - notification │  │  └─────────────────────────────┘  │\n│  └────────────────┘  │  ┌─────────────────────────────┐  │\n│                      │  │  Socket.IO Handlers          │  │\n│  ┌────────────────┐  │  │  - message:send/receive     │  │\n│  │ Services       │  │  │  - dm:send/receive/typing   │  │\n│  │ - api.ts       │  │  │  - sync:request/response    │  │\n│  │ - socket.ts    │  │  │  - quest/milestone notifies │  │\n│  └────────────────┘  │  └─────────────────────────────┘  │\n│                      │  ┌─────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  Pages:              │  │  Modules                    │  │\n│  /dashboard, /chat,  │  │  - AI (Groq system prompts) │  │\n│  /shop, /messages,   │  │  - Chat (sendMessage flow)  │  │\n│  /quests, /memories, │  │  - Character (mood, facts)  │  │\n│  /leaderboard,       │  │  - Quest, Gift, Scene       │  │\n│  /settings/*,        │  │  - Memory, DM, Leaderboard  │  │\n│  /auth/*, /admin     │  │  - Payment (Stripe)         │  │\n│                      │  │  - Analytics, Monitoring    │  │\n└──────────────────────┴──┴─────────────────────────────┘  │\n                           ┌──────────┬──────────────────┘\n                           │PostgreSQL│ Redis\n                           └──────────┴──────────────────┘\n```\n\n**Key interaction patterns:**\n- Client → Server via REST API (`ApiClient` class with auto-refresh on 401, BroadcastChannel cross-tab sync)\n- Client ↔ Server via Socket.IO (real-time chat, typing, notifications, DMs)\n- Server → AI via Groq API (OpenAI-compatible SDK, rich Vietnamese system prompt)\n- Server → Redis for caching (auth, leaderboard, dedup, rate limiting, proactive notifications)\n- Server → PostgreSQL via Prisma (25+ models)\n\n---\n\n### 4. Key Features and Modules\n\n| Module | Features |\n|--------|----------|\n| **Auth** | Register (OTP email verify), login, logout, refresh tokens, forgot/reset password, email verification |\n| **Character** | Create/customize AI companion, personality (5 types), mood system, avatar customization (hair, eyes, skin, outfit, accessories), character templates, relationship stages (8 levels), character facts (AI memory), templates CRUD |\n| **Chat** | Real-time AI chat, paginated history, search, typing indicators, mood/affection changes, optimistic UI, message dedup, AI evaluation of user messages |\n| **AI Engine** | Groq/OpenAI, rich Vietnamese system prompt with personality, relationship stage, affection level, time-of-day context, occupation-based dialogue, pronoun adaptation (gender-aware), fact extraction, forbidden topic handling, quality scoring |\n| **Quests** | Daily/Weekly/Story/Achievement/Event/Relationship quests, progress tracking, reward claiming (XP, coins, gems, affection), premium gating |\n| **Gifts/Shop** | Shop with 5 rarity tiers (Common→Legendary), buy with coins/gems, send to character → AI reaction → affection boost, gift history, limited-time items, premium gating |\n| **Scenes** | Unlockable environments (indoor/outdoor/romantic/etc.), unlock by level/purchase/quest/relationship, active scene setting |\n| **Memories** | Milestone tracking, auto-generated memories (stage change, level up, conversation), favorites gallery |\n| **DM** | User-to-user messaging, 1-on-1 + group chats (3-50 members), typing indicators, read receipts, soft delete, unread count |\n| **Leaderboard** | Rankings by level, affection, streak, achievements, 5-min cache refresh |\n| **Game** | Daily login rewards, streak tracking, progress system |\n| **Analytics** | Usage stats, monitoring telemetry |\n| **Admin** | Admin panel with pricing/tier configuration |\n| **Payment** | Stripe subscriptions (4 tiers: FREE/BASIC/PRO/ULTIMATE), monthly/yearly billing, webhook handling, payment history |\n| **Notifications** | System, chat, quest, achievement, gift, event, reward notifications, proactive AI messages (morning/night/miss_you/anniversary) |\n| **Monitoring** | Request/error/auth/socket/job/security/business event tracking, metric rollups |\n| **Upload** | File upload to DigitalOcean Spaces (multer + S3) |\n\n---\n\n### 5. Data Models / Database Schema\n\n**25+ Prisma models:**\n\n| Model | Key Fields |\n|-------|-----------|\n| **User** | id, email, password, username, displayName, isPremium, premiumTier (FREE/BASIC/PRO/ULTIMATE), coins, gems, streak, userGender, datingPreference, stripeCustomerId |\n| **UserSettings** | userId, language, theme, notifications/sound/music, chatBubbleStyle, fontSize, privacy settings, activeSceneId |\n| **Character** | userId, name, personality, mood, level, experience, affection (0-1000), relationshipStage (8 stages), avatar customization (style, hair, eyes, skin, outfit), AI params (memoryEnabled, responseStyle, creativityLevel), templateId |\n| **CharacterTemplate** | name, description, avatarUrl, gender, personality, style, isDefault, isActive |\n| **CharacterFact** | characterId, category, key, value, importance (1-10), factType (permanent/evolving/temporal), sourceType (manual/ai_inline/ai_batch) |\n| **CharacterScene** | characterId, sceneId, unlockedAt |\n| **CharacterScene** | characterId, sceneId, unlockedAt |\n| **Message** | userId, characterId, role (USER/AI/SYSTEM), content, messageType (TEXT/IMAGE/VOICE/GIFT/STICKER/EVENT), emotion |\n| **ConversationSummary** | userId, characterId, summary, keyTopics, emotionalTone, messageCount |\n| **Quest** | title, type, category, requirements (JSON), rewards (XP/coins/gems/affection), requiresPremium, minimumTier |\n| **UserQuest** | userId, questId, progress, maxProgress, status (IN_PROGRESS/COMPLETED/CLAIMED/EXPIRED) |\n| **Gift** | name, emoji, category, rarity (5 tiers), priceCoins, priceGems, affectionBonus, requiresPremium, minimumTier |\n| **UserGift** | userId, giftId, quantity |\n| **GiftHistory** | userId, characterId, giftId, message, reaction |\n| **Scene** | name, category, ambiance, unlockMethod (level/purchase/quest/event/relationship), unlockValue, requiredStage, priceGems, requiresPremium |\n| **Memory** | userId, characterId, title, type (MILESTONE/PHOTO/CONVERSATION/GIFT/EVENT/SPECIAL/DATE/CHAT), isAutoGenerated, isFavorite |\n| **Achievement** | name, category, requirement (JSON), rewards, points, isSecret |\n| **UserAchievement** | userId, achievementId, progress, unlockedAt |\n| **Notification** | userId, type, title, message, data, isRead |\n| **DailyReward** | userId, day (1-7), rewardType, rewardValue, claimedAt |\n| **Conversation** | isGroup, name (for groups) |\n| **ConversationMember** | conversationId, userId, role (admin/member), lastReadAt, isActive |\n| **DirectMessage** | conversationId, senderId, content, messageType, isDeleted |\n| **RelationshipHistory** | userId, characterId, eventType, fromStage, toStage, note, metadata |\n| **Subscription** | userId (unique), stripeSubscriptionId, tier, billingCycle, status, currentPeriodEnd, cancelAtPeriodEnd |\n| **PaymentHistory** | userId, stripePaymentIntentId, amount (VND int), currency, status, tier, billingCycle |\n| **PasswordResetOTP** | email, otp, type (PASSWORD_RESET/REGISTRATION), expiresAt, used |\n| **RefreshToken** | userId, token, expiresAt, isRevoked |\n| **MonitoringEvent** | eventType, metricKey, severity, source, userId, userTier, path, method, statusCode, durationMs, metadata |\n| **MonitoringMetricRollup** | bucketStart, bucketSize, metricKey, dimensions, count, sumValue, avgValue, p95/p99 values |\n| **AIPromptTemplate** | name, personality, template, systemRole, isActive |\n| **SystemConfig** | key, value (JSON) |\n\n**Key Enums:** Gender, UserGender, DatingPreference, RelationshipStage (8 stages), PremiumTier (4 tiers), MessageRole, MessageType, QuestType, QuestStatus, Rarity (5 tiers), MemoryType, NotificationType, OTPType, BillingCycle, SubscriptionStatus, MonitoringEventType\n\n---\n\n### 6. Authentication & Authorization\n\n**Flow:**\n1. **Register:** POST `/api/auth/register` → OTP sent via email (Nodemailer SMTP) → POST `/api/auth/verify-registration` with OTP → returns JWT tokens\n2. **Login:** POST `/api/auth/login` → returns JWT tokens\n3. **Token Refresh:** POST `/api/auth/refresh` → cookie-based refresh token → new access token\n4. **Password Reset:** POST `/api/auth/forgot-password` → OTP email → POST `/api/auth/verify-otp` → POST `/api/auth/reset-password`\n\n**JWT:**\n- Access token: 15min expiry, Bearer in Authorization header\n- Refresh token: 7day expiry, stored in DB (RefreshToken model), cookie-based\n- Stored in Zustand persist store (localStorage) with key `vgfriend-auth`\n- Cross-tab sync via BroadcastChannel + storage event listener\n\n**Auth Middleware:**\n- JWT Bearer verification with Redis cache-aside (15min TTL)\n- Falls back to DB if cache miss\n- Admin middleware: separate admin auth with `ADMIN_JWT_SECRET`\n\n**Rate Limiting:**\n- Public routes (auth): 100 req / 15min per IP\n- Authenticated routes: 200 req / 1min per user (JWT-based key)\n- Socket: message (10/10s), DM (20/60s), typing (30/60s) per user\n- Nginx: 10 req/s on `/api`, 30 req/s on `/`\n\n**Premium Gating:**\n- PremiumTier enum: FREE, BASIC, PRO, ULTIMATE\n- Quests, gifts, scenes, and shop items can require minimum tier\n- Premium middleware enforces tier requirements\n- Stripe integration for subscriptions\n\n---\n\n### 7. API Endpoints\n\n| Route | Module | Key Endpoints |\n|-------|--------|---------------|\n| `/api/auth` | Auth | POST /register, /login, /refresh, /logout, /forgot-password, /verify-otp, /reset-password, /verify-registration, GET /me |\n| `/api/users` | Users | GET /profile, /settings, PATCH /settings, GET /privacy, PATCH /privacy |\n| `/api/character` | Character | GET/POST/PATCH / (CRUD), /customize, /facts, /templates (public), /relationship |\n| `/api/chat` | Chat | GET /messages (paginated), POST /send, /search |\n| `/api/quests` | Quests | GET /all, /daily, POST /claim/:questId |\n| `/api/gifts` `/api/shop` | Gifts | GET / (shop catalog), /inventory, POST /buy, /send |\n| `/api/scenes` | Scenes | GET / (list), POST /unlock, /set-active |\n| `/api/memories` | Memories | GET / (list), POST / (create), PATCH /:id (favorite), DELETE /:id |\n| `/api/game` | Game | GET /daily-login, /progress |\n| `/api/analytics` | Analytics | GET /stats |\n| `/api/dm` | Direct Messages | GET/POST /conversations, GET/POST /conversations/:id/messages, GET /unread-count |\n| `/api/leaderboard` | Leaderboard | GET /:category (level, affection, streak, achievements) |\n| `/api/admin` | Admin | Admin-only endpoints for pricing/tier config |\n| `/api/payment` | Payment | Stripe webhook, subscription management |\n| `/api/config/tier-plans` | Config | GET (public) - dynamic premium plan configs |\n| `/health` | Health | GET - DB + Redis health check (cached 5s) |\n| `/ready` | Readiness | GET - orchestrator readiness check |\n\n---\n\n### 8. Deployment Setup\n\n**Development:**\n```\ndocker-compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d\n→ PostgreSQL (5432), Redis (6379), Adminer (8080)\nServer: npm run dev (tsx watch, port 3001)\nClient: npm run dev (Next.js, port 3000)\n```\n\n**Production (Docker Compose):**\n- 5 services: postgres, redis, server, client, nginx (profile: production)\n- Images built and pushed to GHCR (`ghcr.io/{repo}/server`, `ghcr.io/{repo}/client`)\n- Nginx handles SSL termination, gzip, rate limiting, WebSocket proxy\n- Health checks on postgres, redis, server\n\n**CI/CD Pipeline (GitHub Actions):**\n1. **Type-check** (Ubuntu, Node 20, `tsc --noEmit`)\n2. **Build & Push Server** (Docker Buildx, GHCR, parallel with client)\n3. **Build & Push Client** (Docker Buildx, GHCR, parallel with server)\n4. **Deploy to VPS** (SSH via appleboy/ssh-action):\n   - Write `.env` from secrets\n   - `docker compose pull`\n   - Start postgres + redis, wait healthy\n   - Run `prisma migrate deploy`\n   - Run `prisma db seed`\n   - `docker compose --profile production up -d --force-recreate`\n   - Verify server healthy (20 retries, 5s each)\n   - Background cleanup (old images, containers)\n\n**Release:**\n- semantic-release with conventional commits\n- Beta releases on `dev` branch, production on `main`\n- Automated CHANGELOG.md updates, GitHub releases\n\n**VPS Requirements:**\n- Ubuntu 20.04+, 1GB RAM min (2GB recommended)\n- Domain: vgfriend.io.vn\n- SSL: Let's Encrypt via certbot\n\n---\n\n### 9. Current Documentation Structure\n\n**`docs/` directory:** EMPTY (no files)\n\n**Documentation that exists:**\n- `README.md` — Comprehensive setup, deployment, API, WebSocket docs\n- `CODEBASE.md` — AI reference codebase summary\n- `CLAUDE.md` / `AGENTS.md` — AI agent workflow instructions (boilerplate from ClaudeKit)\n- `GEMINI.md` — MCP proxy instructions (boilerplate, not VGfriend-specific)\n- `CHANGELOG.md` — Mostly ClaudeKit boilerplate changelog (not VGfriend-specific)\n\n**`plans/` directory:**\n- `reports/` — Tester validation reports for AI naturalness (2026-04-06, 2026-04-07)\n- `templates/` — Bug fix, feature implementation, refactor templates + usage guide\n\n**`guide/` directory:**\n- `COMMANDS.md`, `COMMANDS.yaml` — ClaudeKit command reference\n- `SKILLS.md`, `SKILLS.yaml` — ClaudeKit skills reference\n- `ENVIRONMENT_RESOLVER.md` — Environment resolution guide\n\n**`.claude/rules/` directory:**\n- `primary-workflow.md` — Code implementation workflow (plan → research → code → test → review)\n- `development-rules.md` — Development standards\n- `orchestration-protocol.md` — Agent orchestration protocol\n- `documentation-management.md` — Doc management rules\n- `team-coordination-rules.md` — Team coordination rules\n\n**Notable gap:** The `docs/` folder specified in CLAUDE.md is empty — no architecture docs, code standards, or deployment guides exist yet.\n\n---\n\n### 10. Unique/Interesting Technical Decisions\n\n1. **Vietnamese-first AI with gender-aware pronouns:** The AI system prompt dynamically adapts pronouns based on character gender + user gender combinations (female→male: em/anh, male→female: anh/em, same-gender: mình/cậu). This is sophisticated for a Vietnamese language AI.\n\n2. **Affection-based dialogue tiers (0-1000):** 6 affection tiers with distinct behavior patterns, pet names, and language formality — from formal \"bạn\" to intimate \"anh yêu của em\".\n\n3. **Time-of-day context injection:** The system prompt injects current time period (morning/afternoon/evening/night/latenight) with appropriate greetings and activities, making the AI feel more alive.\n\n4. **Occupation-based roleplay:** 8 occupations (student, office_worker, teacher, nurse, artist, developer, sales, freelancer) each with unique dialogue patterns, hobbies, and roleplay styles.\n\n5. **Character facts system with decay types:** Facts are categorized as permanent (never decay), evolving (slow decay), or temporal (fast decay) — mimicking real memory retention curves.\n\n6. **Message deduplication via Redis setNX:** Uses atomic `setNX` operations with `dedup:{userId}:{clientId}` keys to prevent duplicate message processing on retries.\n\n7. **Cross-tab sync without BroadcastChannel overkill:** Socket.IO room-based broadcast handles same-user multi-tab sync; BroadcastChannel is only used for token sync and localStorage changes.\n\n8. **Optimistic UI with clientId replacement:** Client adds temp message immediately with clientId, server echoes back with real message — client replaces optimistic by matching clientId.\n\n9. **Typing delay proportional to response length:** `Math.min(4000, Math.max(1500, responseLength * 25))` — longer AI responses take longer to \"type\", adding realism.\n\n10. **Stripe integration with VND integer amounts:** Payment amounts stored as integers in VND (no decimals), matching Vietnamese currency conventions.\n\n11. **DigitalOcean Spaces (Singapore region):** S3-compatible storage configured for `sgp1` endpoint with bucket `haichu`.\n\n12. **Per-user rate limiting via JWT decode:** Instead of IP-based limiting for authenticated routes, the server decodes JWT to extract userId and uses `user:{userId}` as the rate limit key.\n\n13. **Conversation summaries for long-term memory:** The `ConversationSummary` model stores AI-generated summaries of past conversations with key topics and emotional tone — used in AI context for long-term recall.\n\n14. **Proactive AI notifications with debounce:** AI can proactively send morning/night/miss-you/anniversary messages, debounced at 5 minutes per user with Redis caching.\n\n15. **Playwright E2E with API + UI tests:** 10 test specs covering auth, chat, dashboard, onboarding — both API-level and UI-level tests.\n\n---\n\n### Unresolved Questions\n\n1. **Shared types package not actively used:** The `@vgfriend/shared` package exists but the server imports directly from `@prisma/client` and the client defines its own types. It's unclear if the shared types are actually consumed by either package.\n\n2. **CHANGELOG.md is stale:** The changelog is entirely from the ClaudeKit boilerplate template, not reflecting actual VGfriend development history.\n\n3. **docs/ folder empty:** Despite being referenced in CLAUDE.md and development rules, the docs folder contains zero files. Architecture diagrams, code standards, and deployment guides don't exist.\n\n4. **Seed data not examined:** The `prisma/seed.ts` file was not read — it likely contains important default data (character templates, quests, gifts, scenes, achievements).\n\n5. **Premium feature gating implementation details:** The premium middleware exists but its exact enforcement logic wasn't examined.\n\n6. **Admin panel functionality:** The admin module has pricing and tier-config controllers but the full admin flow wasn't explored.\n\n7. **AI service truncation:** The `ai.service.ts` file was truncated at 640/988 lines — the actual chat processing logic, emotion detection, and response parsing wasn't fully read."
